### Go

 Exception Type | URLs 
 --- | --- 
 ``` parse : invalid URL escape "%" ```  |  ``` D:///% ```  <br> ``` file://[::]/.////////% ```  <br> ``` https://%@E ```  <br> ``` http://[::]/%2e./% ```  <br> ``` file:///.//% ```  <br> 
 ``` parse .//%: invalid URL escape "%" ```  |  ``` C:/ < .//% ```  <br> 
 ``` parse : net/url: invalid userinfo ```  |  ``` ws://:Ô∫å@H ```  <br> ``` ws://:Ôπ®@E ```  <br> 
 ``` parse : invalid character "}" in host name ```  |  ``` F://"} ```  <br> ``` file://&} ```  <br> ``` B://} ```  <br> ``` file://I} ```  <br> ``` ws://S} ```  <br> 
 ``` parse : invalid character "`" in host name ```  |  ``` ftp://`, ```  <br> ``` T://G` ```  <br> ``` L://` ```  <br> ``` file://;` ```  <br> ``` file://`' ```  <br> 
 ``` parse ///.///%: invalid URL escape "%" ```  |  ``` Z:/ < ///.///% ```  <br> 
 ``` parse : invalid character "{" in host name ```  |  ``` wss://B{ ```  <br> ``` https://{ ```  <br> ``` I://{ ```  <br> ``` file://{ ```  <br> 
 ``` parse /%2e///%: invalid URL escape "%" ```  |  ``` file:/// < /%2e///% ```  <br> 
 ``` parse //}: invalid character "}" in host name ```  |  ``` https://[::] < //} ```  <br>
